| Lake Titicaca                         |  520 |    2 |    1 |  754 |

what are the five above columns?

- The "full name" of each area, followed by four integers
- the area identifier (IAID)
- the area type (IATY)
  1. land/water
  2. continents
  3. countries
  4. states
  5. climate divisions
- a suggested color index, from 1 to 7, inclusive (ISCI)
- the area identifier of the area's "parent", which contains it (IPAR)
